#### FeedQeWhu 
[**`Results`**](./results.md#feedqewhu), [**`Participants`**](./participants.md#whu), [**`Input`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/input.FeedQeWhu.gz), [**`Summary`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.FeedQeWhu), [**`Appendix`**](https://trec.nist.gov/pubs/trec17/appendices/blog/FeedQeWhu.pdf) 

- :material-rename: **Run ID:** FeedQeWhu 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-group: **Participant:** WHU 
- :material-format-text: **Track:** Blog 
- :material-calendar: **Year:** 2008 
- :material-upload: **Submission:** 8/10/2008 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-gear: **Type:** automatic 
- :material-text-search: **Task:** feed 
- :material-fingerprint: **MD5:** `cc755f0bed53103d4cdfb3e6ddea2896` 
- :material-text: **Run description:** Merged the feed documents in different days according to their feednos into a large document as the individual documents in indexing, using Terrier. Using topic titles and an expanded seed ,for each topic, gathering from Wikipedia and Delicious, to retrieve relevant feed documents. The retrieval model is PL2 implemented in Terrier. For each topic, combine the weight of the topic title in returned feeds as well as the weight of expanding queries in their returned feeds, according to a special proportion. Then combing the weight of feeds and rank the feednos, submitting the first 100 here. 

---

#### kunlpKLtdOc 
[**`Results`**](./results.md#kunlpkltdoc), [**`Participants`**](./participants.md#ku), [**`Proceedings`**](./proceedings.md#a-hybrid-method-for-opinion-finding-task-kunlp-at-trec-2008-blog-track), [**`Input`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/input.kunlpKLtdOc.gz), [**`Summary (opinion)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.opinion.kunlpKLtdOc.gz), [**`Summary (topicrel)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.topicrel.kunlpKLtdOc.gz), [**`Appendix`**](https://trec.nist.gov/pubs/trec17/appendices/blog/kunlpKLtdOc.opinion.pdf) 

- :material-rename: **Run ID:** kunlpKLtdOc 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-group: **Participant:** KU 
- :material-format-text: **Track:** Blog 
- :material-calendar: **Year:** 2008 
- :material-upload: **Submission:** 7/2/2008 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-gear: **Type:** automatic 
- :material-text-search: **Task:** opinion 
- :material-fingerprint: **MD5:** `4ef879f8213720e34631935f5a39be95` 
- :material-text: **Run description:** This run is generated based on baseline "kunlpKLtd". Firstly, SVM classifier determines if a blog post  (in corresponding ad-hoc retrieval results) is opinionated or not. Secondly, SVM classifier's output scores of opinionated blog post are linearly combined with topic relevant scores and lexical proximity scores to produce the final re-ranking scores. Features for SVM classifier are opinion words collected from several resources. 

---
#### kunlpKLtdOs 
[**`Results`**](./results.md#kunlpkltdos), [**`Participants`**](./participants.md#ku), [**`Proceedings`**](./proceedings.md#a-hybrid-method-for-opinion-finding-task-kunlp-at-trec-2008-blog-track), [**`Input`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/input.kunlpKLtdOs.gz), [**`Summary (opinion)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.opinion.kunlpKLtdOs.gz), [**`Summary (topicrel)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.topicrel.kunlpKLtdOs.gz), [**`Appendix`**](https://trec.nist.gov/pubs/trec17/appendices/blog/kunlpKLtdOs.opinion.pdf)

- :material-format-text: **Track:** Blog 
- :material-calendar: **Year:** 2008 
- :material-upload: **Submission:** 7/2/2008 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-gear: **Type:** automatic 
- :material-text-search: **Task:** opinion 
- :material-fingerprint: **MD5:** `af63bc5d4a38328e9b9f44056d5c14e8` 
- :material-text: **Run description:** This run is generated based on baseline "kunlpKLtd". SVM classifier is employed to classify blog posts into opinionated or non-opinated class. Only opinionated ones were retained for re-ranking. The re-ranking scores are the linear combination of SVM's output scores and topic relevant scores.

#### kunlpKLtdPs 
[**`Results`**](./results.md#kunlpkltdps), [**`Participants`**](./participants.md#ku), [**`Proceedings`**](./proceedings.md#a-hybrid-method-for-opinion-finding-task-kunlp-at-trec-2008-blog-track), [**`Input`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/input.kunlpKLtdPs.gz), [**`Summary (negative)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.negative.kunlpKLtdPs.gz), [**`Summary (positive)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.positive.kunlpKLtdPs.gz), [**`Appendix (Negative Polarity)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/pubs/trec17/appendices/blog/kunlpKLtdPs.negative.polarity.pdf), [**`Appendix (Positive Polarity)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/pubs/trec17/appendices/blog/kunlpKLtdPs.positive.polarity.pdf) 

- :material-rename: **Run ID:** kunlpKLtdPs 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-group: **Participant:** KU 
- :material-format-text: **Track:** Blog 
- :material-calendar: **Year:** 2008 
- :material-upload: **Submission:** 7/2/2008 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-gear: **Type:** automatic 
- :material-text-search: **Task:** polarity 
- :material-fingerprint: **MD5:** `e1ab5d73105ef5557461cde45acdfc83` 
- :material-text: **Run description:** This run is generated from "kunlpKLtdOc". A ternary SVM classifier is trained from the last 2 years' assessments. It's then used to classify opinionated posts into positive, negative or mixed class. Positive and negative ones were retained for re-ranking. The re-ranking scores are linear combination of SVM's output scores and opinion retrieval scores.

- :material-text: **Run description:** The result is generated by a open toolkit LEMUR. We index all terms including stopwords, and doesn't stem them. Retrieval model is KL, and no query expasion is processed.

#### PermMeWhu 
[**`Results`**](./results.md#permmewhu), [**`Participants`**](./participants.md#whu), [**`Input`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/input.PermMeWhu.gz), [**`Summary`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.PermMeWhu), [**`Appendix`**](https://trec.nist.gov/pubs/trec17/appendices/blog/PermMeWhu.pdf) 

- :material-rename: **Run ID:** PermMeWhu 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-group: **Participant:** WHU 
- :material-format-text: **Track:** Blog 
- :material-calendar: **Year:** 2008 
- :material-upload: **Submission:** 8/10/2008 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-gear: **Type:** automatic 
- :material-text-search: **Task:** feed 
- :material-fingerprint: **MD5:** `c728a96b11c5ce5f4aa37cd9339d9bd6` 
- :material-text: **Run description:** Indexing all the permalinks with Terrier and retrieval all those relevant blog posts using topic titles. The retrieval model is PL2 implemented in Terrier. Within the return 1000 permalinks, those belong to a same feed are combined to get a weight to rank the feednos. 100 feeds with most high weight are submitted here.

#### PermQeWhu 
[**`Results`**](./results.md#permqewhu), [**`Participants`**](./participants.md#whu), [**`Input`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/input.PermQeWhu.gz), [**`Summary`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.PermQeWhu), [**`Appendix`**](https://trec.nist.gov/pubs/trec17/appendices/blog/PermQeWhu.pdf) 

- :material-rename: **Run ID:** PermQeWhu 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-group: **Participant:** WHU 
- :material-format-text: **Track:** Blog 
- :material-calendar: **Year:** 2008 
- :material-upload: **Submission:** 8/10/2008 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-gear: **Type:** automatic 
- :material-text-search: **Task:** feed 
- :material-fingerprint: **MD5:** `c75dc9a0508204bbd627edbfc1c3bb08` 
- :material-text: **Run description:** Indexing all the permalinks with Terrier and retrieval all those relevant blog posts using topic titles and an expanded seed ,for each topic, gathering from Wikipedia and Delicious. The retrieval model is PL2 implemented in Terrier. For each topic, combine the weight of the topic title in returned permalinks as well as the weight of expanding queries in their returned permalinks  according to a special proportion. Then combing the weight of all permalinks belong a same feeds and rank the feednos, submitting the first 100 here. 

---

#### uams08nonr 
[**`Results`**](./results.md#uams08nonr), [**`Participants`**](./participants.md#uams_de_rijke), [**`Proceedings`**](./proceedings.md#external-query-expansion-in-the-blogosphere), [**`Input`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/input.uams08nonr.gz), [**`Summary`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.uams08nonr), [**`Appendix`**](https://trec.nist.gov/pubs/trec17/appendices/blog/uams08nonr.pdf) 

- :material-rename: **Run ID:** uams08nonr 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-group: **Participant:** UAms_De_Rijke 
- :material-format-text: **Track:** Blog 
- :material-calendar: **Year:** 2008 
- :material-upload: **Submission:** 8/9/2008 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-gear: **Type:** automatic 
- :material-text-search: **Task:** feed 
- :material-fingerprint: **MD5:** `06b9038841caf78707ff1c4c9493856f` 
- :material-text: **Run description:** We use an expert retrieval model; the association values are estimated based on blog specific features like number of comments, post length, and posting time. Finally, we enhance presicion by combining the run with a title-only run. This final score indicates the relevance of a blog; besides this relevance we also estimate non-relevance using the average retrieval score per blog over the 2007 topics. Dividing the relevant by the non-relevant score gives us the final retrieval score. 

---

- :fontawesome-solid-user-group: **Participant:** UAms_De_Rijke 
- :material-format-text: **Track:** Blog 
- :material-calendar: **Year:** 2008 
- :material-upload: **Submission:** 8/9/2008

- :material-text-search: **Task:** feed 
- :material-fingerprint: **MD5:** `3d996754d0f83a4552d2295f32ddaee2`

#### uicirwa 
[**`Results`**](./results.md#uicirwa), [**`Participants`**](./participants.md#uic_ir_group), [**`Proceedings`**](./proceedings.md#uic-at-trec-208-blog-track), [**`Input`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/input.uicirwa.gz), [**`Summary (opinion)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.opinion.uicirwa.gz), [**`Summary (topicrel)`**](https://trec.nist.gov/results/trec17/blog/summary.topicrel.uicirwa.gz), [**`Appendix`**](https://trec.nist.gov/pubs/trec17/appendices/blog/uicirwa.baseline.pdf) 

- :material-rename: **Run ID:** uicirwa 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-group: **Participant:** UIC_IR_Group 
- :material-format-text: **Track:** Blog 
- :material-calendar: **Year:** 2008 
- :material-upload: **Submission:** 6/10/2008 
- :fontawesome-solid-user-gear: **Type:** automatic 
- :material-text-search: **Task:** baseline 
- :material-fingerprint: **MD5:** `7beb9b31a04f4224276c8fd12d4e8383` 
- :material-text: **Run description:** The run is obtained by a concept-based information retrieval system. Each document's similarity consists of a phrase similarity and a term similarity. Each query is tried to retrieved a synonym in wikipedia. Moreover, we utilize three methods of query expansions, web feed back, wikipedia feed back and pseudo feed back. For each query, it is retrieved on the basis of concept in the query, query terms and 20 epansion terms.

- :material-text: **Run description:** This method incorporates our method B strategy which re-ranks documents only by sentiment weights, except incorporating the tf-idf formula for each document. The tf-idf formula is isolated to *sentiment* terms found in the document only. No target terms are considered in this run, as future runs (other methods) will incorporate target terms as well.
